<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отливать.html>отлива́ть</a> (11445)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отлить.html>отли́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otlítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отливать.html>отлива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otlivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отлить.html>отли́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pour off, to pump out</li>
<li>to found, to cast</li>
<li>to flow back, to ebb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take a leak, to make water</li>
<li>to be shot <i>(with a colour)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отливать.html>отлива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красный.html>кра́сным</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:зеленый.html>зелёным</a>)</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otlivátʹ</b> krásnym (zeljónym)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">be shot with red (green)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>лить</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">litʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отлить.html>отли́в</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otlív</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отливка.html>отли́вка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otlívka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:литье.html>литьё</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">litʹjó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***отлить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отлить.html>отли́ть</a> (13054)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">litʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отлить.html>отли́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otlítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отливать.html>отлива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pour off, to pump out</li>
<li>to found, to cast</li>
<li>to flow back, to ebb
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>кровь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отлить.html>отлила́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> кого́-либо</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krovʹ <b>otlilá</b> ot licá u kovó-libo</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">smb's face paled [grew pale; turned bloodless; went white]</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take a leak, to make water</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличать.html>отлича́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otličávšij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличить.html>отличи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otličítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличать.html>отлича́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otličátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличить.html>отличи́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отличаться.html>отлича́ться</a> (1600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличать.html>отлича́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otličátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличаться.html>отлича́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otličátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличиться.html>отличи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to differ (<a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> - from) <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">not to have the same characteristics</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to be notable <i>(for)</i></li>
<li>to distinguish oneself, to excel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">disapprovable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make an exhibition of oneself</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличать.html>отлича́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otličátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отличаться.html>отличающийся</a> (1600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличаться.html>отлича́ющийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otličájuščijsja</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличаться.html>отлича́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otličátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ча<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ю<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>щий<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отличие.html>отли́чие</a> (1892)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличие.html>отли́чие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otlíčije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличие.html>отли́чия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличие.html>отли́чия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличие.html>отли́чий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>difference (quality of being different)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отличие.html>отли́чие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:европейский.html>европе́йских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́н</a> - экономи́чность</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Otlíčije</b> jevropéjskix mašín - ekonomíčnostʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">European cars stand out by being economical</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>distinction
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медаль.html>меда́ль</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>За</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отличие.html>отли́чие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:служба.html>слу́жбе</a>»</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">medálʹ “Za <b>otlíčije</b> v vojénnoj slúžbe”</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">medal for distinguished military service</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make an exhibition of oneself</li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отложение.html>отложе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otložénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отложение.html>отложе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отложение.html>отложе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отложение.html>отложе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deposit; sediment, sedimentation, precipitation, deposition</li></ol>

***отложить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отложить.html>отложи́ть</a> (3514)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отложить.html>отложи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otložítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откладывать.html>откла́дывать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отлага́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to set aside</li>
<li>to lay by, to save (money for some purchase)</li>
<li>to put off, to delay, to adjourn, to postpone</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lay <i>(eggs, spawn etc.)</i></li>
<li>to fold/turn back</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отлупить.html>отлупи́ть</a> (25254)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лупить.html>лупи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отлупить.html>отлупи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otlupítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лупить.html>лупи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to thrash, to flog, to spank, to beat, to batter</li>
<li>to beat, to drub, to clobber</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лу<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ча́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отлучить.html>отлучи́ть</a> (24706)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">лучи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lučítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to unite (originally, to separate)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отлучить.html>отлучи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otlučítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отлуча́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to separate, to remove</li>
<li>to exclude, to excommunicate, to ostracize, to shun
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отлучить.html>отлучи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:церковь.html>це́ркви</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otlučítʹ</b> ot cérkvi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to excommunicate</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***отмахать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отмахать.html>отмаха́ть</a> (29183)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмахать.html>отмаха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmaxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отма́хивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to signal with a flag</li>
<li>to finish waving</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмахать.html>отмаха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmaxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отма́хивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cover, to travel (a distance)

<li>to wave away</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ма<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ха́ть</b>
